SENTIENT SPECIES:
Grey Koboldoids with Giant Eyes: Eat pretty much anything, including one another. Disturbingly fond of skulls. They have grey skin. They have bilateral symmetry. Their giant eyes take up most of their head. They are gregarious and unwilling to compromise. They first evolved on Bylox II in 694.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: -1 CON: 1 INT: -1 CHA: -1
Amorphous Koboldoids: Eat pretty much anything, including one another. Disturbingly fond of skulls. They have bilateral symmetry and are able to greatly alter their shape. They are fond of practical jokes and have a deep need to conform. They first evolved on Eilat IV in 689.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 2 CON: 3 INT: 1 CHA: -3
Feathered Red Trolloids: They have lost the ability to reproduce naturally, and compensate for this with a focus on science and paranoia. They have red feathers. They have bilateral symmetry. They are violent and have a complex system of social castes. They were uplifted by the Republic of Koboldoids and Trolloids on Autorog V in 717.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -1 CON: 0 INT: 1 CHA: 2
Telepathic Blue Deep Dwellers: They live in the deep oceans or in deep caves, hiding. Their presence can go unnoticed for a long time. They have blue skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They can read each others' minds. They are humorless and strive to uphold their ideals of personal honour. They developed from Flying Blue Deep Dwellers in 721.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -2 CON: 2 INT: 1 CHA: 0
Tiny White Trolloids with Five-fold Symmetry: They have lost the ability to reproduce naturally, and compensate for this with a focus on science and paranoia. They have white skin. They have five-fold symmetry. They are humorless and have a complex system of social rules. They developed from Tiny White Trolloids with Threefold Symmetry in 652.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -2 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: -1

CIVILISATIONS:
THE REPUBLIC OF KOBOLDOIDS AND TROLLOIDS:
An ancient, fantastically wealthy, advanced Republic of 19 planets, with 65 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
25 billion Amorphous Koboldoids.
8 billion Tiny White Trolloids with Five-fold Symmetry.
7 billion enslaved Grey Koboldoids with Giant Eyes.
15 billion enslaved Feathered Red Trolloids.
10 billion enslaved Telepathic Blue Deep Dwellers.
It controls a Artificial Plague.
It controls a Master Computer.

	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 0 CON: 2 INT: -1 CHA: 1

WE ENTER THE FIRST AGE OF CIVILISATION
68:
The population of Scaly Antoids on Dekuv IV has grown by a billion.
Gas bags evolve on Fynot III.
69:
The population of Scaly Antoids on Dekuv IV has grown by a billion.
The Empire of Giant Koboldoids explore Urbon I. 
70:
The Empire of Giant Koboldoids uplift the local Flying Dwarfoids on Autorog V and incorporate the planet into their civilisation.
Brain parasites evolve on Metatron IV.
71:
The population of Giant Koboldoids on Urbon I has grown by a billion.
The population of Scaly Antoids on Dekuv IV has grown by a billion.
Sentient Yellow Koboldoids arise on Fynou III.
72:
The population of Giant Koboldoids on Urbon I has grown by a billion.
The Empire of Giant Koboldoids explore Orgus I. The expedition encounters brain parasites. Upon their return to Urbon I, the parasites take over the brains of the planet's inhabitants, creating the Kingdom of Parasites.
The Empire of Giant Koboldoids attack Urbon I, a colony of the Kingdom of Parasites, and subject it to orbital bombardment, killing 3 billion.
73:
The Empire of Giant Koboldoids attack and raze Urbon I, a colony of the Kingdom of Parasites.
The Kingdom of Parasites collapses.
74:
The population of Giant Koboldoids on Autorog V has grown by a billion.
Overcrowding on Autorog V leads to increased pollution.
The Empire of Giant Koboldoids build a mining base on Cilat IV.
75:
The Yellow Koboldoids on Fynou III mutate into Scaly Yellow Koboldoids.
The population of Scaly Antoids on Dekuv IV has grown by a billion.
Radiovores evolve on Eilat IV.
76:
The population of Flying Dwarfoids on Autorog V has grown by a billion.
The population of Giant Koboldoids on Autorog V has grown by a billion.
The population of Scaly Antoids on Dekuv IV has grown by a billion.
The Scaly Antoids on Dekuv IV achieve spaceflight and organise as a Theocracy, the Church of Scaly Antoids.
